 jammu-kashmir main pidipi or bijepi kii gathbandhan sarkaar girane ke baad rajya main rajyapal shashan lagu ho gaya he
 The state is under Governor's rule for the eighth time so far

 He held a meeting with the state's senior administrative officials and security forces officers in Srinagar on Wednesday

 He is the only governor appointed during the Congress government which has not been removed by the BJP government

 Governor's rule is enforced in the state for six months under Section 92 of the Constitution of Jammu and Kashmir, although this can only happen after the President's approval
 bharat kaa samvidhan jammu -kashmir ko vishesh darja pradaan karata he or yah desh kaa ekmaatr aisa rajya he jiske paas alag samvidhan or niyam hai
